 #  Ceil : [real](https://github.com/PlasmaEngine/PlasmaDocs/blob/master/code_reference/lightning_base_types/real.markdown)

 `static`

> Rounds value upward. The place represents where in the number we want to perform rounding (0 is the 1s place, 1 is the 10s place, -1 is the tenths place, etc).
> |Name|Type|Description|
> |---|---|---|
> |value|[real](https://github.com/PlasmaEngine/PlasmaDocs/blob/master/code_reference/lightning_base_types/real.markdown)| |

> function Ceil(value : Real, places : Integer) : Real
> ```

 #  Floor : [real](https://github.com/PlasmaEngine/PlasmaDocs/blob/master/code_reference/lightning_base_types/real.markdown)

 `static`

> Rounds value downward. The place represents where in the number we want to perform rounding (0 is the 1s place, 1 is the 10s place, -1 is the tenths place, etc).
> |Name|Type|Description|
> |---|---|---|
> |value|[real](https://github.com/PlasmaEngine/PlasmaDocs/blob/master/code_reference/lightning_base_types/real.markdown)| |

 #  Floor : [real2x3](https://github.com/PlasmaEngine/PlasmaDocs/blob/master/code_reference/lightning_base_types/real2x3.markdown)

 `static`

> Rounds value downward. The place represents where in the number we want to perform rounding (0 is the 1s place, 1 is the 10s place, -1 is the tenths place, etc). Performed component-wise.
> |Name|Type|Description|
> |---|---|---|
> |value|[real2x3](https://github.com/PlasmaEngine/PlasmaDocs/blob/master/code_reference/lightning_base_types/real2x3.markdown)| |
> |places|[integer](https://github.com/PlasmaEngine/PlasmaDocs/blob/master/code_reference/lightning_base_types/integer.markdown)| |
> |numericalBase|[integer](https://github.com/PlasmaEngine/PlasmaDocs/blob/master/code_reference/lightning_base_types/integer.markdown)| |
> ``` lang=cpp, name=Lightning
> function Floor(value : Real2x3, places : Integer, numericalBase : Integer) : Real2x3
> ```

> |---|---|---|

> ```

 `static`

> Linearly interpolates from start to end by the fraction t. T of 0 is start and t of 1 is end.

> |---|---|---|
> |start|[real](https://github.com/PlasmaEngine/PlasmaDocs/blob/master/code_reference/lightning_base_types/real.markdown)| |
> |end|[real](https://github.com/PlasmaEngine/PlasmaDocs/blob/master/code_reference/lightning_base_types/real.markdown)| |

> ``` lang=cpp, name=Lightning
> function Lerp(start : Real, end : Real, t : Real) : Real
> ``` 


---  
 #  Lerp : [real2](https://github.com/PlasmaEngine/PlasmaDocs/blob/master/code_reference/lightning_base_types/real2.markdown)

---  
 #  Lerp : [real4x3](https://github.com/PlasmaEngine/PlasmaDocs/blob/master/code_reference/lightning_base_types/real4x3.markdown)

 `static`

> Linearly interpolates from start to end by the fraction t. T of 0 is start and t of 1 is end. Performed component-wise.
> |Name|Type|Description|
> |---|---|---|
> |start|[real4x3](https://github.com/PlasmaEngine/PlasmaDocs/blob/master/code_reference/lightning_base_types/real4x3.markdown)| |
> |end|[real4x3](https://github.com/PlasmaEngine/PlasmaDocs/blob/master/code_reference/lightning_base_types/real4x3.markdown)| |
> |t|[real](https://github.com/PlasmaEngine/PlasmaDocs/blob/master/code_reference/lightning_base_types/real.markdown)| |

> function Lerp(start : Real4x3, end : Real4x3, t : Real) : Real4x3
> ```

 #  Max : [integer](https://github.com/PlasmaEngine/PlasmaDocs/blob/master/code_reference/lightning_base_types/integer.markdown)

 `static`

> Returns whichever value is larger.
> |Name|Type|Description|

 #  Multiply : [integer2](https://github.com/PlasmaEngine/PlasmaDocs/blob/master/code_reference/lightning_base_types/integer2.markdown)

 `static`

> Multiplies the two matrices together. Matrix multiplication is in right-to-left order, that is if the matrices represent transformations, then 'the' is applied first followed by 'by'.
> |Name|Type|Description|
> |---|---|---|
> |by|[integer2x2](https://github.com/PlasmaEngine/PlasmaDocs/blob/master/code_reference/lightning_base_types/integer2x2.markdown)| |
> |the|[integer2](https://github.com/PlasmaEngine/PlasmaDocs/blob/master/code_reference/lightning_base_types/integer2.markdown)| |
> ``` lang=cpp, name=Lightning
> function Multiply(by : Integer2x2, the : Integer2) : Integer2
> ```

> |the|[integer3](https://github.com/PlasmaEngine/PlasmaDocs/blob/master/code_reference/lightning_base_types/integer3.markdown)| |
> ``` lang=cpp, name=Lightning
> function Multiply(by : Integer3x3, the : Integer3) : Integer3
> ``` 


---  
 #  Multiply : [integer3x2](https://github.com/PlasmaEngine/PlasmaDocs/blob/master/code_reference/lightning_base_types/integer3x2.markdown)

 `static`

> Multiplies the two matrices together. Matrix multiplication is in right-to-left order, that is if the matrices represent transformations, then 'the' is applied first followed by 'by'.
> |Name|Type|Description|
> |---|---|---|
> |by|[integer3x3](https://github.com/PlasmaEngine/PlasmaDocs/blob/master/code_reference/lightning_base_types/integer3x3.markdown)| |

> Multiplies the two matrices together. Matrix multiplication is in right-to-left order, that is if the matrices represent transformations, then 'the' is applied first followed by 'by'.
> |Name|Type|Description|
> |---|---|---|
> |by|[real2x4](https://github.com/PlasmaEngine/PlasmaDocs/blob/master/code_reference/lightning_base_types/real2x4.markdown)| |
> |the|[real4x3](https://github.com/PlasmaEngine/PlasmaDocs/blob/master/code_reference/lightning_base_types/real4x3.markdown)| |
> ``` lang=cpp, name=Lightning
> function Multiply(by : Real2x4, the : Real4x3) : Real2x3
> ```

> |p0|[real4](https://github.com/PlasmaEngine/PlasmaDocs/blob/master/code_reference/lightning_base_types/real4.markdown)| |
> ``` lang=cpp, name=Lightning
> function Round(p0 : Real4) : Real4
> ``` 


---  
 #  Round : [real4](https://github.com/PlasmaEngine/PlasmaDocs/blob/master/code_reference/lightning_base_types/real4.markdown)

 `static`

> Returns the integer value closest to value. The place represents where in the number we want to perform rounding (0 is the 1s place, 1 is the 10s place, -1 is the tenths place, etc). Performed component-wise.
> |Name|Type|Description|
> |---|---|---|
> |value|[real4](https://github.com/PlasmaEngine/PlasmaDocs/blob/master/code_reference/lightning_base_types/real4.markdown)| |
> |places|[integer](https://github.com/PlasmaEngine/PlasmaDocs/blob/master/code_reference/lightning_base_types/integer.markdown)| |
> ``` lang=cpp, name=Lightning
> function Round(value : Real4, places : Integer) : Real4
> ```

 #  SlerpUnnormalized : [real2](https://github.com/PlasmaEngine/PlasmaDocs/blob/master/code_reference/lightning_base_types/real2.markdown)

 `static`

> Spherical linear interpolation. Used to interpolate between two vectors by the parameter t. This is the 'pure' mathematical Slerp function that works on un-normalized input. This effectively traces along an ellipse defined by the two input vectors.
> |Name|Type|Description|
> |---|---|---|
> |start|[real2](https://github.com/PlasmaEngine/PlasmaDocs/blob/master/code_reference/lightning_base_types/real2.markdown)| |
> |end|[real2](https://github.com/PlasmaEngine/PlasmaDocs/blob/master/code_reference/lightning_base_types/real2.markdown)| |
> |t|[real](https://github.com/PlasmaEngine/PlasmaDocs/blob/master/code_reference/lightning_base_types/real.markdown)| |
> ``` lang=cpp, name=Lightning
> function SlerpUnnormalized(start : Real2, end : Real2, t : Real) : Real2
> ```

 #  Transpose : [boolean2x2](https://github.com/PlasmaEngine/PlasmaDocs/blob/master/code_reference/lightning_base_types/boolean2x2.markdown)

 `static`

 #  Truncate : [real4x3](https://github.com/PlasmaEngine/PlasmaDocs/blob/master/code_reference/lightning_base_types/real4x3.markdown)

 `static`

---  
 #  Truncate : [real4x3](https://github.com/PlasmaEngine/PlasmaDocs/blob/master/code_reference/lightning_base_types/real4x3.markdown)

 `static`

> Rounds value towards plasma. The place represents where in the number we want to perform rounding (0 is the 1s place, 1 is the 10s place, -1 is the tenths place, etc). Performed component-wise.
> |Name|Type|Description|
> |---|---|---|
> |value|[real4x3](https://github.com/PlasmaEngine/PlasmaDocs/blob/master/code_reference/lightning_base_types/real4x3.markdown)| |
> |places|[integer](https://github.com/PlasmaEngine/PlasmaDocs/blob/master/code_reference/lightning_base_types/integer.markdown)| |
> ``` lang=cpp, name=Lightning
> function Truncate(value : Real4x3, places : Integer) : Real4x3
> ```
